src="/img/graduation-cap-icon.svg" alt="" class="academyIcon_l_RD"></span></div></div></ul></li><li class="theme-doc-sidebar-item-category theme-doc-sidebar-item-category-level-1 menu__list-item 0"></path><path d="M19.98 10.023c0 .2-.058.399-.168.547l-4.996 7.492a.987.987 0 01-.828.454h-3c-.547 0-.996-.453-.996-1 0-.2.059-.403.168-.551l4.625-6.942-4.625-6.945a.939.939 0 01-.168-.55 1 1 0 padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_z5aJ"><div class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/search"><span>How-to: Query &amp; Search</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Hybrid search</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Hybrid search</h1></header><p><code>Hybrid</code> search combines the results of a vector search and a keyword (BM25F) search by fusing the two result sets.</p>
<p>The <a href="#change-the-fusion-method" class="">fusion method</a> and the <a href="#balance-keyword-and-vector-search" class="">relative weights</a> are configurable.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>Prefer natural language queries?</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>The <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/query-agent">Query Agent</a> translates plain English questions into optimized Weaviate queries automatically - no manual query construction needed.</p><span class="cloudOnlyBadge_iHZd compact_l2tC"><img src="/img/cloud-icon.svg" alt="" class="cloudIcon_a1CI"><span>Cloud only</span></span></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="basic-hybrid-search">Basic hybrid search<a href="#basic-hybrid-search" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic hybrid search" title="Direct link to Basic hybrid search" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Combine the results of a vector search and a keyword search. The search uses a single query string.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="named-vectors">Named vectors<a href="#named-vectors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Named vectors" title="Direct link to Named vectors" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.24</code></div></div>
<p>A hybrid search on a collection that has <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#named-vectors">named vectors</a> must specify a <code>target</code> vector. Weaviate uses the query vector to search the target vector space.</p>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Example response</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>The output is like this:</p><div><div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-json codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2"></div></div></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="explain-the-search-results">Explain the search results<a href="#explain-the-search-results" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Explain the search results" title="Direct link to Explain the search results" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>To see the object rankings, set the <code>explain score</code> field in your query. The search rankings are part of the object metadata. Weaviate uses the score to order the search results.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="balance-keyword-and-vector-search">Balance keyword and vector search<a href="#balance-keyword-and-vector-search" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Balance keyword and vector search" title="Direct link to Balance keyword and vector search" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Hybrid search results can favor the keyword component or the vector component. To change the relative weights of the keyword and vector components, set the <code>alpha</code> value in your query.</p>
<ul>
<li class="">An <code>alpha</code> of <code>1</code> is a pure vector search.</li>
<li class="">An <code>alpha</code> of <code>0</code> is a pure keyword search.</li>
</ul>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option><option value="graphql">GraphQL</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="change-the-fusion-method">Change the fusion method<a href="#change-the-fusion-method" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Change the fusion method" title="Direct link to Change the fusion method" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p><code>Relative Score Fusion</code> is the default fusion method starting in <code>v1.24</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li class="">To use the keyword and vector search relative scores instead of the search rankings, use <code>Relative Score Fusion</code>.</li>
<li class="">To use <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/additional-operators#autocut"><code>autocut</code></a> with the <code>hybrid</code> operator, use <code>Relative Score Fusion</code>.</li>
</ul>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary><p>Additional information</p></summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>For a discussion of fusion methods, see <a href="https://weaviate.io/blog/hybrid-search-fusion-algorithms" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">this blog post</a> and <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/search-operators#variables-2">this reference page</a></p></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="keyword-search-operators">Keyword search operators<a href="#keyword-search-operators" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Keyword search operators" title="Direct link to Keyword search operators" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.31</code></div></div>
<p>Keyword (BM25) search operators define the minimum number of query <a href="#tokenization" class="">tokens</a> that must be present in the object to be returned. The options are <code>and</code>, or <code>or</code> (default).</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="or"><code>or</code><a href="#or" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to or" title="Direct link to or" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>With the <code>or</code> operator, the search returns objects that contain at least <code>minimumOrTokensMatch</code> of the tokens in the search string.</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="and"><code>and</code><a href="#and" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to and" title="Direct link to and" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>With the <code>and</code> operator, the search returns objects that contain all tokens in the search string.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-keyword-search-properties">Specify keyword search properties<a href="#specify-keyword-search-properties" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify keyword search properties" title="Direct link to Specify keyword search properties" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.19.0</code></div></div>
<p>The keyword search portion of hybrid search can be directed to only search a subset of object properties. This does not affect the vector search portion.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="set-weights-on-property-values">Set weights on property values<a href="#set-weights-on-property-values" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Set weights on property values" title="Direct link to Set weights on property values" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Specify the relative value of an object&#x27;s <code>properties</code> in the keyword search. Higher values increase the property&#x27;s contribution to the search score.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-a-search-vector">Specify a search vector<a href="#specify-a-search-vector" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify a search vector" title="Direct link to Specify a search vector" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>The vector component of hybrid search can use a query string or a query vector. To specify a query vector instead of a query string, provide a query vector (for the vector search) and a query string (for the keyword search) in your query.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option><option value="graphql">GraphQL</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="vector-search-parameters">Vector search parameters<a href="#vector-search-parameters" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Vector search parameters" title="Direct link to Vector search parameters" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.25</code></div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Note that the hybrid threshold (<code>max_vector_distance</code>) was introduced later in <code>v1.26.3</code>.</p></div></div>
<p>You can specify <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/similarity">vector similarity search</a> parameters similar to <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/similarity#search-with-text">near text</a> or <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/similarity#search-with-a-vector">near vector</a> searches, such as <code>group by</code> and <code>move to</code> / <code>move away</code>. An equivalent <code>distance</code> <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/similarity#set-a-similarity-threshold">threshold for vector search</a> can be specified with the <code>max vector distance</code> parameter.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="hybrid-search-thresholds">Hybrid search thresholds<a href="#hybrid-search-thresholds" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Hybrid search thresholds" title="Direct link to Hybrid search thresholds" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.25</code></div></div>
<p>The only available search threshold is <code>max vector distance</code>, which will set the maximum allowable distance for the vector search component.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. Check the<!-- --> <a href="/weaviate/release-notes">Release notes</a> <!-- -->for specific versions.<br><br>If a snippet doesn&#x27;t work or you have feedback, please open a<!-- --> <a href="https://github.com/weaviate/docs/issues/new?template=doc_feedback.yml&amp;title=%5BDocumentation+Feedback%5D%3A+&amp;labels=user-feedback&amp;page-url=" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">GitHub issue</a>.</span></span></span></div></div></div><div class="codeContent_E0WP"><div class="tabPanel_nEcw" style="display:block" aria-hidden="false"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><div><div class="language-python codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="group-results">Group results<a href="#group-results" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Group results" title="Direct link to Group results" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.25</code></div></div>
<p>Define criteria to group search results.</p>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Example response</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>The response is like this:</p><div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_e6Vv"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">&#x27;Jeopardy!&#x27;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">&#x27;Double Jeopardy!&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></details>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="limit--offset"><code>limit</code> &amp; <code>offset</code><a href="#limit--offset" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to limit--offset" title="Direct link to limit--offset" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>limit</code> to set a fixed maximum number of objects to return.</p>
<p>Optionally, use <code>offset</code> to paginate the results.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="limit-result-groups">Limit result groups<a href="#limit-result-groups" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Limit result groups" title="Direct link to Limit result groups" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>To limit results to groups with similar distances from the query, use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/additional-operators#autocut"><code>autocut</code></a> filter. Specify the <code>Relative Score Fusion</code> ranking method when you use autocut with hybrid search.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Autocut requires <code>Relative Score Fusion</code> method because it uses actual similarity scores to detect cutoff points. Autocut shouldn&#x27;t be used with <code>Ranked Fusion</code> as this fusion method relies on ranking positions, not similarity scores.</p><p>To learn more about the different fusion algorithms, visit the <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/search-operators#fusion-algorithms">search operators reference page</a>.</p></div></div>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="filter-results">Filter results<a href="#filter-results" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Filter results" title="Direct link to Filter results" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>To narrow your search results, use a <a class="" href="/weaviate/api/graphql/filters"><code>filter</code></a>.</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="tokenization">Tokenization<a href="#tokenization" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Tokenization" title="Direct link to Tokenization" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<!-- -->
<p>Weaviate converts filter terms into tokens. The default tokenization is <code>word</code>. The <code>word</code> tokenizer keeps alphanumeric characters, lowercase them and splits on whitespace. It converts a string like &quot;Test_domain_weaviate&quot; into &quot;test&quot;, &quot;domain&quot;, and &quot;weaviate&quot;.</p>
<p>For details and additional tokenization methods, see <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#tokenization">Tokenization</a>.</p>
